# Synopsis

- Caden finds a pomegranate and a secret cypher letter.
- Cas and Eloise train after Cas does a recon of the castle.
- Eszter Kovács is head of the Tested in Montimer. Writes a letter to Sov and Lyla, granting her "permission" to release the intel on Sazed's child. She wants a supervised visit at an inn at "noon."
- Audry gathers the gang.
- Peter is able to tell that the room's geometry does not support "secret/false walls" for spies. Lyla does hear water draining, but it's PROBABLY from the kitchens above draining the water from sinks, etc.
- "We are here but it is too dangerous to meet you. We will try to meet when it is safer."
- "We are here, but it is too dangerous to meet. We will try to meet you when it is safer." -- note left on the pomegranate.
- Using Decipher, Peter attempts to backward engineer the code language to leave a message back to them. He has to keep it to roughly ten characters.
- They are meeting tomorrow at 12, or 3 days at dusk.
- They are all going to the meeting with Sazed's child.
- Eszter Kovács, head/Ematha of the Tested in Montimer.
- She IS, in fact, Blue. That is not a trick of the light or an off-reflection in Estin. She has a mixed heritage of something. She herself serves those of us who attended the meeting, giving specific - well-selected options - to individuals.
- The troupe hears something most of them have only heard of -- the chime of a clock striking noon.
- Tabitha van der Meer, an Estin woman, greets the group.
- She is the mother!
- She is a single-ring Tested. She has a daughter who's roughly 3.
- Tabitha is a diplomat to House Lumia, a Mikado Estine house.
- Lyla gives her a rock, Emily gives back a branch (with a leaf).
- Emily Songwillow.
- We are all absolutely charmed by little Emily Songwillow.
- She says Lyla's baby is "between the tears."
- Emily is a magic baby.
- She rests her hand against Casimir's belly too and said you lost something too - but you wanted to lose it.
- She goes to Peter and says how he's lost his mother. So Emily hugs Peter, because he misses his mom.
- Emily goes further to say to Siobhan that not everyone likes to meet her/talk to her because she can "see inside of people."
- After a lot of sassy spicy back and forth, Eszter flips a coin out onto the table. "That's why I wanted to have the Heir of Selene and Sir MacBravo in the same room." On one side of the coin is a sigil of House Rivers, the other the Crest of Sedi - as the House Rivers was a banner to Sedi. When Lyla questions her own inclusion, being of neither of these things - Eszter clarifies: well, because you each (Lyla and Peter) each carry the heirs of both.
